remarks:
remarks:        Contact for peering requests is:
remarks:
remarks:        peering@netcologne.de
remarks:
remarks:
remarks:        Contact for criminal use and spam reports is:
remarks:
remarks:        abuse@netcologne.de
remarks:
remarks:
remarks:        Engineering Communities
remarks:
remarks:        NetCologne customers are allowed to use a set of
remarks:        predefined communities to influence the announcement
remarks:        of their prefixes at specific IXes.
remarks:
remarks:        8422:10xxy public peerings
remarks:        8422:15xxy private peerings
remarks:        8422:19xxy upstreams
remarks:
remarks:        where xx defines where and y defines what to do.
remarks:
remarks:        8422:1000y all public peerings
remarks:        8422:1001y DE-CIX
remarks:        8422:1002y AMS-IX
remarks:        8422:1003y LINX
remarks:        8422:1006y ECIX DUS
remarks:        8422:1009y ECIX FFM
remarks:
remarks:        8422:1500y all private peerings
remarks:        8422:1508y AS20773 (Host Europe)
remarks:        8422:1509y AS15169 (Google)
remarks:        8422:1511y AS20676 (QSC)
remarks:
remarks:        8422:1900y all upstreams
remarks:        8422:1901y AS3356 (Colt)
remarks:        8422:1902y AS1299 (Arelion)
remarks:        8422:1905y AS174 (Cogent)
remarks:        8422:1906y AS9002 (RETN)
remarks:
remarks:
remarks:        y = 0 announce without any prepends
remarks:        y = 1 prepend 1 x AS8422
remarks:        y = 2 prepend 2 x AS8422
remarks:        y = 3 prepend 3 x AS8422
remarks:        y = 9 do not announce
remarks:
remarks:        More specific communities will override less specific
remarks:        communities; e.g. setting 8422:10009 8422:10010 means
remarks:        do not announce at any public peering except DE-CIX.
remarks:        In case of any question regarding this functionality
remarks:        please contact peering@netcologne.de.
